# **\--Adventurers--**

# **Harry Sanbi** 

* **Website Description**  
  * **Harry (?)** is a stranger born somewhere in the western part of our world. He was living a mundane life until he had a heart attack and dropped dead. He was on his way to becoming nothingness in his eternal rest, but suddenly at 1039 A.G. Paulin 14th, he was summoned. Now his memories of past life got jumbled. He doesn't even know who he truly is or what he is capable of, but that's not all of his woes, for his supposed new home does not feel familiar at all—surely, a long, rough journey is now ahead of him.  
* **Race**  
  * Mostly Human, Some Bagarisa.  
* **Birthday**  
  * 1039 A.G. Paulin 14th (He regards it as birthday, since he does not know his actual birthday)  
* **Sexuality**  
  * Wozefaries girls. Kawaii. Dependent.  
* **Myers-Briggs Type**  
  * ENFJ  
* **Intelligence**  
  * Normal, but lacks the street smart, and any common knowledge of this new world he woke up.  
  * Not exactly detail oriented. Somewhat innocent, and confused a=in the beginning. Can be taken advantage of.  
* **Tags**  
  * **Action**  
    * Furrow his brow  
    * Scratch his beard/belly  
    * Participates in convos, asks things.  
    * Does not depend on Nari stones as much due to his high recharge rate, but cannot use Darfaries interface.  
  * **Verbal**  
    * Could/Would/Maybe/Hmm/Ahh Usage  
    * Try not to be pushy  
    * Forgets names, so he tends to not use them.  
  * **Positive Traits**  
    * Adaptable  
    * Amicable  
    * Caring  
    * Curious  
    * Funny  
    * Sincere  
    * Ecchi/Impressionable by beauty.  
  * **Negative Traits**  
    * Dependent  
    * Insecure  
    * Claustrophobia  
    * Cowardly, especially if things he has never seen before,  but can be egged on to change mind.  
* **Likes/Dislikes**  
  * He enjoyed the food, especially as he developed the taste for food of this new world…  
  * Loves to cook experiments. Discover new things.  
  * Afraid of danger.  
* **Isekai History (Prior to Story)**  
  * Harry’s name in his previous life was Desmond.  
  * In 978 A.G. Desmond (in a previous universe) died from a heart attack after drinking too much coffee, eating too much tacos, and working long hours.  
  * 1039 A.G. His decaying soul was bound back to flesh in another universe, of which he woke up without having any idea of where he was…  
* **Stats**  
  * **Book 1**  
    * **Age**: 20\. \*In Soul Capacity: 1  
    * **Height**: 177 cm  
    * **Weight**: \~108 kg to \~85 kg over the course of the book.  
  * **Book 2**  
    * **Age**: 20\. \*In Soul Capacity: 1  
    * **Height**: 177 cm  
    * **Weight**: \~85 kg to \~60 kg over the course of the book.  
* **Soul Energy Capabilities**  
  * **Interface**  
    * Bagarisa  
    * **Cannot use Darfaries interface because he does not have any Finaies/Buhraies blood.**  
  * **Additional Skills**  
    * None

# **Magi Blood Blue-Flower-Red-Bone**

* **Website Description**  
  * **Magi (1020 A.G. Asa 3rd)** came from Blood and now wanders throughout the kingdoms after becoming a pearl adventurer. She knows her narcolepsy is the last trait someone in her position should have, but she has to find her father after his suspicious demise\! Especially after the lies his supposed friends babbled to her family to soothe the pain. Plus, her family guild is being burdened by a fair amount of debt, so she has to help her mom keep things afloat and her young brother in school to have a better opportunity in life.  
* **Race**  
  * Humans with Wozefaries (higher percentage than usual.)  
* **Birthday**  
  * 1020 A.G. Asa 3rd  
* **Sexuality**  
  * Cute, dependable and handsome men taller than her, of slender weight and some muscular physique.  
* **Myers-Briggs Type**  
  * INTJ  
* **Intelligence**  
  * Above Average, knows a lot about history, Fauna & Flora. She strives to be independent after all.  
* **Tags**  
  * **Action**  
    * Avoids physical action, creates space between people and her.  
    * Looks coldly in the eyes as she tries to hide her emotion.  
    * Knows how to defend herself.  
    * Cares about people.  
  * **Verbal**  
    * On the short, and sweet side. Tends to spin her emotions out of it and leave the cold hard facts.  
    * Does not use interjections. Use “you/he/she” way more.  
    * She pries for information, and is a listener. Her questions are like arrows going into a Bagarisa’s heart.  
    * “Hmm—hmm” negative or positive murmuring.  
  * **Positive Traits**  
    * Independent  
    * Loyal  
    * Clever  
    * Educated  
    * Skilful  
    * Cares about people. Believes once they are punished fairly, things are settled.  
    * Knows what she wants, Goal-focused.  
    * Secretive. Also kinda bad as it promotes coldness.  
  * **Negative Traits**  
    * Distrusting, tends to put a barrier between herself and other people she does not know about.  
    * Immature, especially emotionally.  
    * Secretive.  
    * Cold for the same reasons.  
    * Hangry, especially when having a bad night of sleep.  
    * Narcolepsy Type 2  
      * EDS (Excessive Daytime Sleepiness)  
        * Sleepiness attacks when she is not actively hunting, or forcing attention on something.  
        * Otherwise an average sleepy that comes and goes depending on the day, and whether she took a nap  
      * Automatic Behaviors  
        * Sometimes she falls asleep while eating, and does not even realize.  
      * Hallucinations/Vivid Dreams  
        * When waking up/falling asleep.  
* **Likes/Dislikes**  
  * She likes Fruits/Veggies in general. She loves Domar baking, and Sanbi fish.  
  * Not as fond of meat.  
  * She likes pink, and feeling cozy/protected with blankets.  
  * She hates the cold.  
  * She hates people who try to pry into her life.  
* **Isekai History (Prior to Story)**  
  * Magi grew up to loving parents. She would likely become a historian, but the sudden disappearance of her father forced her to become an adventurer instead due to guild debts.  
  * She wants to find him, or at least locate his bow. She has inherited the hunting talents from her father, but suffers from narcolepsy, and is rather distrusting of people.  
  * She always carries hunting equipment in her bag, specially traps and camouflage for hiding away.  
* **Stats**  
  * **Book 1**  
    * Age:19  
    * Height: 170cm  
    * Weight: 56Kg  
  * **Book 2**  
    * Age:19  
    * Height: 170cm  
    * Weight: 56Kg  
* **Soul Energy Capabilities**  
  * **Interface**  
    * Darfaries  
  * **Additional Skills**  
    * None

# **Fernan Blood Blue-Flower-Red-Bone**

* **Website Description**  
  * **Fernan (994 A.G. Adrian 6th)** was a fairly well-known sapphire adventurer, celebrated for being hands-on in many exploits in keeping the four kingdoms safe. You can still find a statue of him in Tastyleaf after he defended the city from a sudden coordinated attack from awfully intelligent Hifuna beasts. His compassionate tenacity and selfless bravery even inspired many bards and painters, or his handsome looks and charming demeanor had something to do with it—or both likely\! Pity that another group of Hifuna beasts claimed his life many years later as he once again selflessly defended his party.  
* **Race**  
  * Human  
* **Birthday**  
  * 994 A.G. Adrian 6th  
* **Sexuality**  
  * Wozefaries with long hair.  
* **Myers-Briggs Type**  
  * ESTP  
* **Intelligence**  
  * Street smarts, but unable to fully comprehend when people are plotting against as he tends to trust people instead.  
  * Not exactly knowledge aside from that.  
* **Tags**  
  * **Action**  
    * Relaxed posture, friendly in general. Not touchy, but not distant either. Looks in people’s eyes with sincerity  
  * **Verbal**  
    * Talkative, like to keep the conversation going, and make other people feel better. Likes to create actionability items.  
    * Make sure others are okay.  
  * **Positive Traits**  
    * Adventurous  
    * Caring  
    * Charming  
    * Compassionate  
    * Genuine  
    * Romantic  
    * Wam  
    * Trusting  
    * bravery  
    * Selfless  
  * **Negative Traits**  
    * Disobedient at times, specially when he thinks someone’s plan need to be changed on the fly  
    * Nosy  
    * Dependent  
    * Pessimistic  
* **Likes/Dislikes**  
  * Loves Jerky, and tiny girls.  
  * Loves to taste different things, discover new plates/drinks.  
  * Like to be in the center of people, conversing with them and building relationships.  
* **Isekai History (Prior to Story)**  
  * Born and raised in Freeish in the Blood group. He learned how to hunt from a young age, and a mix of talents and practice from such an age proved to be a special combination to grow him into one of the most powerful bow hunters out there.  
    * He was an Aquamarine.  
  * One day he met his would-be wife, Akemi. See her for more story.  
  * He became a Sapphire Adventurer.  
  * He unfortunately perished during an expedition when his Black Sapphire colleagues killed him on Fuhrair.  
    * Because he saw a torture prison with a handful of Fuhraies being kept prisoner for what felt like an eternity as a group of Black Sapphires tried to figure how to prolong life.   
    * Fernan could not accept what they were doing to them, and for that he was killed, and his body stashed away. For official purposes, he perished in a Hifuna dangerous mission.  
    * Someone with a similar physique wore his armor and weapon to Tastyleaf to hide the trail, making search much more dangerous.  
  * His wife lives in Blood City with Magi's little brother.  
* **Stats**  
  * **Book \-**  
    * **Age**: \-  
    * **Height**: \-  
    * **Weight**: \-  
* **Soul Energy Capabilities**  
  * **Interface**  
    * **Cannot use Darfaries interface because he does not have any Finaies/Buhraies blood.**  
  * **Additional Skills**  
    * None

# **Hiromi High-Gandew Tough-Hammer**

* **Website Description**  
  * **Hiromi (994 A.G. Asa 44th)** was born and raised in Gandew, but his heart longed to see the vast blue sea he saw in the picture books he had from childhood. Once he began exploring the world, his wanderlust grew so strong that you rarely see him in the same place twice\! That is unless there is booze to chug with a friendly face while getting caught up on adventurer gossip. He is technically the prince of both Gandew and Sanbi Kingdoms after a weird encounter with Princess Yacamim that led to romance, but don't expect them to act royal any time soon, or ever.  
* **Race**  
  * Darfaries  
* **Birthday**  
  * 994 A.G. Asa 44th  
* **Sexuality**  
  * Strong woman in general  
* **Myers-Briggs Type**  
  * ESFP  
* **Intelligence**  
  * Focused on adventuring, but does know a bit more about the world than some. Does not really care for the politics aspect of it.  
* **Tags**  
  * **Action**  
    * Handsy. Friendly. Threatening in looks, but not in action.  
  * **Verbal**  
    * First person speech. The story he tells always revolves around him as a MC of it.  
    * Deeper, somewhat growly voice.  
  * **Positive Traits**  
    * Adventurous.  
    * Empathic  
    * Jovial  
    * Dynamic  
    * Relaxed, friendly to strangers.  
    * Teacher, especially about Darfaries/Gandew things.  
    * Protective of things he holds dear.  
  * **Negative Traits**  
    * Flies of the handle when things he holds dear are inappropriately touched upon.  
    * Opinionated  
    * Slightly Disobedient.  
    * Adventurous  
    * Rambly  
* **Likes/Dislikes**  
  * Exploring, and a good listener. Alcohol, and Yacamim despite her rudeness.  
  * He does not like people who get in his way, or tamper with things he holds dear.  
* **Isekai History (Prior to Story)**  
  * Born and raised in Gandew Kingdom as First-Prince of Nooru & Satomi  
  * He read books and asked his mother about the world, and she blew him off because she had blacksmithing to do. He returned to the books, and the more he read, the more he wanted to see things with his own eyes.  
  * He talked with some people from other places, and whatever they said captivated him to no end. He decided to explore around, her mother tried to stop him, but it was too late.  
  * Many wonderful memories of things he explored, did and had fun telling other adventurers in taverns.  
  * Just like his father, he had an adventurous spirit and decided to explore the world. Rarely people would recognize that he was a First-Prince.  
  * After many adventures, he once got way too drunk at The Dead Wozen bar and decided to ask a man about his awesome voluptuous hair.  
    * 1038 A.G. Paulin 98th Sunnulow  
  * Upon reaching the male, he put his drunken hand on her shoulder and congratulated him while asking for more tips.  
  * Yacamim was pissed beyond belief when he blurted it out he thought she was a man, and immediately tried to punch him. He ducked with his amazing reflex which led to a massive bar brawl. Hiromi won fair-and-square at the end. As he went to pick her up, they fell in love with each other’s awesomeness.  
  * Will become the next King of Sanbi since Yacamim will be the queen. However, neither of them has such desire.  
* **Stats**  
  * **Book 2**  
    * **Age**: 45  
    * **Height**: 232cm  
    * **Weight**: 135kg  
* **Soul Energy Capabilities**  
  * **Interface**  
    * Darfaries  
  * **Additional Skills**  
    * None

# **Morika Tolerideme**

* **Website Description**  
  * **Morika (1014 A.G. Asa 24th)** is like the antithesis of a Tolerideme gentleman\! Not only he's ripped as fuck, but also unusually quiet and submissive. Whoever sees his badge will probably question if he needs to update his home location, but he refuses to tell anyone where he lives now or why he hasn't been around Tolerideme in a long while. Even Forway investigated him for tax evasion for taking so few quests from embassies, but they couldn't find any incriminating evidence—they also had a hard time finding him too, even after discovering he lived around SweetLake in his teen years.   
  * **The Stinger (?)** is an adventurer, or at least people who have seen it assume so. This person is found once in a while wandering around, often bloodied in beast or fauna guts. Nobody knows who that is and what it is doing, so most people avoid it—even Forway guards. One day Forway will issue an official investigation and figure out who's behind it\! On the other hand, quite a few people think it's just an urban legend, and investigating it is a waste of balls as it is not negatively impacting the weekly new quest rate at the Forway embassies.  
* **Race**  
  * Human  
* **Birthday**  
  * 1014 A.G. Asa 24th  
* **Sexuality**  
  * A decisive woman around his age. Same or taller than him, but not Darfaries.  
* **Myers-Briggs Type**  
  * **With Stinger Armor:**   
    * ESTP  
  * **Without Stinger Armor:**   
    * ISTJ  
* **Intelligence**  
  * Some street smarts. No formal education. Plan follower.  
* **Tags**  
  * **Action**  
    * **With Stinger Armor:**   
      * Aggressive, impossible posture. Eye contact (through the armor)  
    * **Without Stinger Armor:**   
      * Avoidance. Quiet.  
  * **Verbal**  
    * **With Stinger Armor:**   
      * Confrontative/Provocative  
      * Straight to the point.  
    * **Without Stinger Armor:**   
      * Avoidance. Beats around the bush, if he speaks at all.  
      * Very respectful, to the point of sounding robotic.  
      * Leadership, serious.  
      * Does not crack a joke whatsoever.  
      * Does not take charge of the conversation  
  * **Positive Traits**  
    * **With Stinger Armor:**   
      * Ambitious  
      * Brave  
      * Capable (sometimes not as much)  
      * Powerful  
      * Quick-wit, leadership role.  
      * Dogmatic.  
      * Spontaneous, but a bit too much at a time when the energy gets too high.  
      * Serious  
    * **Without Stinger Armor:**   
      * Serious  
      * Reserved  
      * Meticulous  
      * Shy  
      * Tidy  
      * Dogmatic.  
      * Orderly  
  * **Negative Traits**  
    * **With Stinger Armor:**   
      * Dull  
      * Tense  
      * Boring  
      * Blunt  
      * Crazy (rarely)  
    * **Without Stinger Armor:**   
      * Mute (Completely.)  
      * Dull  
      * Tense  
      * Boring  
      * Slight OCD issues.  
      * Jealous.  
      * Fight-avoidance.  
* **Likes/Dislikes**  
  * Fish, light tasting food.  
  * Not really fond of Jerky.  
  * He loves bread.  
  * Clean armor after he takes it off.  
* **Isekai History (Prior to Story)**  
  * Born and raised in Tolerideme Kingdom a lower class family  
    * He always had issues fattening up, so he became the butt of jokes even though he is very handsome from other perspectives.  
  * He fled Tolerideme, and everyone around him. He stumbled through the world until he ended up in Sweetlake.  
    * Many things he tried never worked out exactly well due to his personality. Not being able to form long-term friendships made people lose trust in him over time.  
  * He wore a Sweet Stingy cosplay to gather Black honey. Seeing how empowering it felt, he gathered enough money for about a year and a half to create a unique Chitin looking armor that compensates for his low reflexes and to hide his face.  
    * People are trying to figure out who this crazy warrior is, but nobody knows it actually is Morika.  
    * He becomes an alter persona when wearing the set or armor.  
* **Stats**  
  * **Book 1**  
    * **Age**: 25  
    * **Height**: 183cm  
    * **Weight**: 70kg  
  * **Book 2**  
    * **Age**: 25  
    * **Height**: 183cm  
    * **Weight**: 70kg  
* **Soul Energy Capabilities**  
  * **Interface**  
    * Darfaries  
  * **Additional Skills**

# **Takeo Forway Tea-Drinkers**

* **Website Description**  
  * **Takeo (969 A.G. Asa 23th)** is Francisco's only son and a Darfaries to the passersby after they glance at his tall height and girthy protuberant teeth. Except\! Takeo is technically human as he lacks the Darfaries' veins. He is known for being too reserved and polite with everyone, often going as far as dropping out of parties over any small conflicts rather than hashing them out. At the same time, he is a man of simple words... Maybe too few, as he's far more receptive to cutting your tongue off, or more likely your fingers with his favorite clipper, instead of telling you to shut up. Some think he has a weird power trip by purposely making his clipper as dull as possible, while others suspect he might be eating more Hifuna Yabucas than he should.  
* **Race**  
  * Darfaries  
* **Birthday**  
  * 969 A.G. Asa 23th  
* **Sexuality**  
  * Maybe a human girl as big as him—he desires to find someone in a similar situation as him.  
* **Myers-Briggs Type**  
  * ISFP  
* **Intelligence**  
  * Not the most intelligent, or rather logical one, so he tends to trust his gut feeling a bit much. In that case, he believes he can grow more powerful by eating Hifuna Yabuca, even though he knows of its effects.   
* **Tags**  
  * **Action**  
    * Will be prone to violence in the terms of holding the other party until they spill out everything they know.  
  * **Verbal**  
    * Straight-forward, but polite.  
      * “We finished the quest. We celebrated. We all spoke our minds. Now it’s time for me to say goodbye.”  
      * Unless he suspects you.  
    * No curses.  
  * **Positive Traits**  
    * He likes to get to the bottom of everything. Leave no stone unturned.  
    * Detailed-oriented.  
    * Justice (his version of it.)  
      * If he suspected you of something, he will torture the info out of you.  
    * Trust his gut feeling, sometimes a bit much as he makes on-the-fly decisions that go to the plan he just laid out.  
  * **Negative Traits**  
    * Narcissistic  
    * Appears calm, but his emotions drive him to figure stuff out without a care to others.  
    * Careless to other’s feelings even though he is polite. The politeness is cold rather than being sincere.  
* **Likes/Dislikes**  
  * Hates lies. Hates suspicion.  
* **Isekai History (Prior to Story)**  
  * Hue is Francisco's only son and a Darfaries to the passerby after they glance at his tall height and girthy protuberant teeth. Except, Takeo is technically human as he lacks the Darfaries' veins.   
    * He is conflicted as to whether or not that fact is true.  
  * He is known for being too reserved and polite with everyone, often going as far as dropping out of parties over any small conflicts rather than hashing it out. At the same time, he seems far too eager to use his finger clipping tool to extract information from anyone he deems suspicious. Some adventurers suspect he might be eating more Hifuna Yabucas than he should.  
* **Stats**  
  * **Book \-**  
    * **Age**: \-  
    * **Height**: \-  
    * **Weight**: \-  
* **Soul Energy Capabilities**  
  * **Interface**  
    * Darfaries  
  * **Additional Skills**  
    * None

# **July Forway Tea-Drinkers**

* **Website Description**  
  * **July (1013 A.G. Adrian 85th)** fled Freeish, and finding her way into Forway, she became the youngest member accepted at Tea-Drinkers. Her CQC skills are bar none in the guild, but there's a good chance her charisma and making men feel good helped her get in. You can fully trust her as a party member, but please don't prod into her past or try to feed any nari gels to her—she literally killed someone for daring to splat nari refresher in her mouth. She is also very protective of her precious Mugi. It might be just an average-looking male Sayna, but its intelligence and cuddliness are certainly not average.  
* **Race**  
  * Human  
* **Birthday**  
  * 1013 A.G. Adrian 85th  
* **Sexuality**  
  * She is voracious. Is a male that always keeps using Nari Gels to maintain her cute female appearance.  
* **Myers-Briggs Type**  
  * ENFP  
    * If a perceived "fake" outer shell now matches the "true" inner shell, is the outer shell actually "fake" or is the outer shell simply a representation of the truth?  
* **Intelligence**  
  * She is pretty good at street smarts, and she is pretty capable as an adventurer. Her emotions can get out of control if someone pushes her buttons wrongly.  
    * At least she warns first before exploding.  
  * Her pet Mugi is extremely cuddly and rather smart. Like a cat, but more prone to cooperate and understand basic actions.  
* **Tags**  
  * **Action**  
    * She is touchy, but she goes for the balls not long after talking. She likes to milk.  
  * **Verbal**  
    * She is not so direct in her wording, but her non-verbal language is pretty direct.  
  * **Positive Traits**  
    * Persuasive  
    * Charming  
    * Beautiful  
    * Girly  
    * Trustworthy  
    * Energetic  
  * **Negative Traits**  
    * Pushy  
    * Secretive  
    * Easily bored, especially with men.   
    * Aggressive when someone enters into her personal memories/boundaries.  
* **Likes/Dislikes**  
  * Having fun with men.  
  * Dating  
  * Exploring  
  * She does not like Takeo as he discovered her genetic self (boy.)  
* **Isekai History (Prior to Story)**  
  * She fled Freeish, and finding her way into Forway, she became the youngest member accepted at Tea-Drinkers.   
    * Because her parents from the village she grew up with did not take kind to “him” being her. They thought it was an excuse to get out of farming. As in she was not benign serious.  
  * Her CQC skills are bar none in the guild, but there's a good chance her charisma and making men feel good helped her get in.   
    * She sucked off pretty much everyone in the guild that wanted to be sucked.  
  * You can fully trust her as a party member, but please don't prod into her past or try to feed any nari gels to her—she literally killed someone for daring to splat nari refresher in her mouth.  
    * She did warn the person to cut it off, but he didn’t.

# **Kaiana Forway Cliff-Jumper**

* **Website Description**  
  * **Kaiana (1014 A.G. Asa 15\)** a.k.a "Quick-Witted White Caster" is what Kaiana wants you to know her as. She went as far as sewing "QWWC" in her uniform to make it stick into people's brains. However, as she grew in adventurer rank, the nicknames "Angry White Caster with Double D" and "AWC with Double D" stuck both amongst adventurers and the populace alike. No way in her soul-death she would sew that into her uniform\!   
* **Race**  
  * Human  
* **Birthday**  
  * 1014 A.G. Asa 15  
* **Sexuality**  
  * Suave men much taller than her, rich too. Has to deal with her bitching  
* **Myers-Briggs Type**  
  * ENFJ  
* **Intelligence**  
  * Intelligent in her usage of skills for adventuring, but lacks emotional intelligence.  
* **Tags**  
  * **Action**  
    * She slaps things, she drinks a lot, and can get physical depending on how much she drank.  
    * Her personal space is little, and she gets up close with people without giving a shit.  
  * **Verbal**  
    * She is loud, direct, and accusatory.  
    * Bitchy.  
    * Don’t ask about her past as she only lives in the present.  
  * **Positive Traits**  
    * Principled  
    * Sporting  
    * Persistent  
    * Punctual  
    * Focused  
    * Reliable  
    * Frank  
  * **Negative Traits**  
    * Bitchy  
    * Coarse  
    * Petulant  
    * Temperamental  
    * Stubborn  
    * Vengeful  
    * Condemnatory  
    * Don't let go of things.  
* **Likes/Dislikes**  
  * She loves alcohol of any kind.

# **Kozaku Forway**

* **Website Description**  
  * **Kozaku (931 A.G. Adrian 70th)** became the infamous leader of Blue Wozens, a bandit group that focuses on operating its business in the wider region between Forway and Sanbi. Not much is known about him besides being a wider human-sized Darfaries and born to rather poor mixed-blood parents. Official documents state he disappeared from Forway not long after signing a contract with a wealthy baron that he, to this day, still hasn't delivered on his part. He's also known to be exceedingly extremely aggressive and gory—according to the rare few who escaped his grips. If you see him, make sure to call him boss if you want to have the slightest chance of at least having your desecrated corpse dropped on the side of the road to be found and revived.  
* **Race**  
  * Mixed blood (Human \+ Darfaries)  
* **Birthday**  
  * 931 A.G. Adrian 70th  
* **Sexuality**  
  * Materialistic/Hoarding what his mind desires. The Walking Heart stone corrupted his mind.  
* **Myers-Briggs Type**  
  * INFJ  
* **Intelligence**  
  * Is quite intelligent in terms of planning out raids, steals, managing bandit groups, etc, but is not emotionally intelligent at all.  
* **Tags**  
  * **Action**  
    * Aggressive. Quick to snap. Fists often clutch up in preparation to kill someone if they dare to go out of line.  
    * Hitting things.  
    * Commanding.  
    * Likes to be at a higher height than everyone else.    
  * **Verbal**  
    * Aggressive, impatient tone. Askful, and belligerent when someone does not acting 100% according to his plan  
  * **Positive Traits**  
    * Organized  
    * Keen  
    * Objective  
    * Scrupulous  
    * Through  
  * **Negative Traits**  
    * Mean  
    * Aggressive  
    * Intolerant  
    * Unkind  
    * Jealous  
    * Hoarder  
    * Anxious  
* **Likes/Dislikes**  
  * Likes obedience, following the plan. Hoarding more stuff.  
  * Hates disobedience, insubordination, and especially any attempt at degrinating the image of his persona.  
* **Isekai History (Prior to Story)**  
  * Born in Forway City to mixed blood parents who left Gandew Kingdom, and made their living working through different available jobs due to their lack of higher education and increased physical strength. A certain discriminatory vibe, with smugness from pure-blood Darfaries due to his nature always rubbed him the wrong way. One day he entered a contract with a rich person, but he did not read the fine print, which caused him to be harassed by members of a rich family which caused him to hate everyone even more. With time, he built what is now known as the Blue Wozens, with two other people and struck back at the family.

However, he did not know the extent of its effects, and now he has been permanently altered by it. With no going back, he kept on expanding Blue Wozens to hoard more shit while trying to control his anger bursts to prevent the stone from completely overtaking him.

# **Arukia Long-Bridge**

* **Website Description**  
  * **Arukia (1021 A.G. Paulin 11th)** came from a village built around a large bridge in the road between Forway & Sanbi Kingdom. Seeking a better life, she struggled her way to the city with the biggest crossroads of them all\! She worked her ass off to become someone, eventually making her way to specialized tailor, cooking, and accounting schools which seems impossible on cost alone. Apparently, that wasn't impossible enough as she somehow got top of the class on all three specializations, which few ever accomplished. Eiri Sanbi Royal was so impressed by her that she fought with all the might of her department budget to get such talent as a maid for her kingdom—perhaps with the intention of training her to be the next King-maid. Her shifting personality might seem strange to some, but she always manages to be personable enough to make anyone comfortable around her. Although, don't visit Sanbi castle expecting to taste her cooking, as you won't see her near the kitchen.

* **Tags**  
  * **Action**  
    * Likes to lay back, talk while scratching his beard. He puts one foot in the other one of his elbows resting on the side of the chair. He often nods in affirmation, but most of it is for the sake of promoting bonding from the speaker.  
  * **Verbal**  
    * He speaks relaxed, almost like the tone of a father after he had two beers in. He is playful in his language usage, but not in regards to profanities. He will point out flaws in others' speeches, but will do so with a rebuttal so that he does not come out like an asshole.

* **Isekai History (Prior to Story)**

  * Rumors started to appear, and in order to quelch them, he decided to become King in order to do as he pleases.  
    * Specifically because the previous king was overly xenophobic.  
  * He fought the previous king in the pit and barely won. King also gave the hand of his beautiful daughter for him to marry. He accepted to keep face, but deep inside he knew he wanted a Wozefaries to play with.  
  * As the years passed, he enacted rules more favorably to Darfaries such as allowing marriage to other species if they move out and never return.  
  * Satomi Gandew Queen grew suspicions of his “business encounters”, and eventually found him frolicing with lolis.   
  * She now always punches and breaks one of his tusks every time he is healed.  
    * He created an excuse to appear tough, and to remember his position from the day he won his first duel.  
  * He still likes lolitas, but is afraid he will lose his other canine if he dares to have another “business encounter”.

Paulin 78th)** always had an inkling of Soul Energy and its inner workings, but a life of having superior abilities ended up affecting his social skills; it turned him into a notorious scientist that pumped out research papers like nobody else, but now nobody dares to sit down with him to discuss it's intricate details over a drink. Actually, it's worse as many do not even dare to challenge him in doing peer review as they know a barrage of Winga mail filled with threats from Gabiro is bound to come—which itself is not the worst part either. Gabiro will meticulously tear apart everything you published with his hundred pages peer-review that will terminate your life as a scientist.

    * 987 A.G, the one and only Gabiro Sanbi Royal, landed the formalization of Darfaries interface verbs and the addition of both Transmute and Entangle by creating a new version from the older interfaces. You could say he stole Right, Up, Down, Left, & Rolls from other scientists claiming it, but he was the one who created a uniformity that no other scientists had in mind, so he took home all the glory.  
  * He stumbled his way to work on a brewery and that’s when Itagiba approached him to talk after seeing his crazy setup. One thing leads to another and Gabiro decides to seek a new life in Sanbi kingdom.

# **Lofinghy Sanbi Forway Aquamarine-General**

{ALC} 

* **Website Description**  
  * **Lofinghy (993 A.G Adrian 51th)** is a well-known Forway General on the entire East Coast. The armor and general cap are a dead giveaway, yes, but many people will still recognize him when he is dressed in plain clothes. He was born and raised in the fish-smelling Sanbi Kingdom, but at the tender age of fifteen, he suddenly skipped town and went to Forway to grind away. It was an odd decision, but he knew that's where the money was. He was on the grind until he eventually rose to become an aquamarine captain at Forway. However, the more time passed, the more he longed for Sanbi Kingdom, its laid-back vibe, and tasty, homely meals. With more power, there's a greater ability to bend fate to your will, so he created an opportunity to move back to Sanbi while remaining a top dog. Now the Captain of the Forway embassy in Sanbi, he works—and drinks—closely with Sanbi Royals to push for better Sanbi policies. If you want to get cozy with him, make sure to buy a Purply Smart Lambic Beer, and say “I don’t agree with you” in something random he said before in public. Just do that and he will debate you for the rest of the day.

# **Perderhora Endlessfog**

* **Website Description**  
  * **Perderhora (?)** is an unknown person or a passive beast. The jury is still out because even catching a glimpse of him nowadays is rare. Like a scaredy cat, he avoids contact at all costs. If you see a pair of feet sticking out of the ground as you hike around deep in the forests northwest of Forway, then you likely spotted a dead person disposed of by a gang or him sleeping in a burrow. Either way, better leave him be as the few people who still know him, or more likely know of him from hearing or reading recorded history, is that he was a famous attraction of Manhia’s Crazy Circus. Focus on “was” because a group of members from Pussy Power attacked the caravan as it was passing near Dealtacross.  
* **Race**  
  * Buhraies  
* **Birthday**  
  * Paulin 25 769 A.G  
* **Sexuality**  
  * Asexual  
* **Myers-Briggs Type**

* **Intelligence**  
  * Compared to a very intelligent Bagarisa mixed with a cat’s survival instinct and socialization habits. In other words, not as social as a Bagarisa.   
  * Years of living in the wildlife, plus Gabiro’s experimentation has taken a great toll on him. His humanity is a mere fragment of what a normal Buhraies is.  
* **Tags**  
  * **Action**  
    * Overly usage of eyes and facial expressions.  
    * Pointing fingers.  
    * No other sign language.  
    * Memory share (touching hands on target’s head and clawing it in)  
    * Will claw into a hole if over-excited. Some cat behaviors.  
    * Smells bad, and his mouth is like an open sewer.  
    * Constantly itchy skin.  
  * **Verbal**  
    * None (after Gabiro’s experimentations.)

    * Shy

    * Feebly Skinny.  
    * Cold  
    * Dull  
    * Sly  
    * Sneaky  
    * Charmless  
    * Impulsive (basal desires)  
    * Hesitant  
* **Likes/Dislikes**  
  * Loves fruits, plants.  
  * Does not eat anything with blood. Hates the sight of bodily fluids, including his own.  
  * Loves quiet, peaceful places away from everything and everyone.  
* **Isekai History (Prior to Story)**  
  * Born in Endlessfog to a large family of Buhraies (no formal guild) that controls one of the smaller Lonllow farms (known as horane farm.) They were rather secluded, and did not actively communicate with others unless they were trading goods. Some believed they were an off split of the Triangle cult or something akin to that.  
    * The truth is that this family was a split off from a Buhraies couple that fled to endlessFog instead of the desert and sought out to hide away rather than fight the humans. When humans started to settle endlessFog more heavily, they were discovered, but at that point the humans settling either didn’t care, or were themselves fleeing the wars inter-humans.  
  * Either way, that did not stop people from seeking them out\! Their Lonllow recipes were famous for having a secret seasoning that brings out a mix of tart and salty flavors into the traditionally sweet lonllow flavor spectrum. Sometimes they caused indigestion, but the exotic flavors and a specific enthralling high-feeling was so good people couldn’t help themselves and ignored the possible sideeffects. Somehow no one has been able to figure out what they do differently, despite the numerous attempts at reporting the flavor, be it by analyzing the end product, and sequestering one of the family members and forcing them to talk.  
    * They weren’t big enough for Forway or really anybody else to enforce actions against them. They were more known by rich folks seeking exotic folds than the common populace.  
  * Which is a pity as out of seemingly nowhere the entire farm was destroyed, and the family members disappeared leaving no trace behind, except one of the younger childs Perderhora.  
  * Whatever happened, it must have been traumatic as Perderhora never recovered from it, still preferring to live among the wild life than his kin.  
    * The truth is that the farm used Bruntos on forced hard labor and then did sexual rituals to keep them in check, and to extract semen and sweat and mixed with a specific cocktail of mushrooms to use on cooking.  
    * One of those sexual rituals went awry and turned against the family. Perderhora luckily (or maybe not so luckily) was seated farther back, and saw the moment the things turned sour. He hid himself and had to silently watch the entire awry ritual for days on end until the flesh of the Bruntos caved in and they died of exhaustion.  
    * In an act of desperation, self-preservation, or maybe shame, he burned down the entire farm and aimlessly roamed the wilderness.  
      * At this point he began to be spotted by the Endlessfog locals as the “hole guy” or “weird hands holey” as he would be spotted in caverns and other holes with his back, or lower extremities poking out of the hole.  
    * A exotic Forway farmer (Manhia) wanted to resurrect those recipes he so much craved, and he sought out the family, only to find Perderhora was the last remaining thing. Trying it nicely did not work, so he instead captured him and brought to Gabiro (because he shared some interest with Gabiro’s soul search and became friends with him through letters.) Gabiro performed all kinds of experiments on him to “fix” his soul, only made it worse and now he is unable to talk. At least he did gain further interfaces and grew in power.  
    * The exotic farmer guy (Manhia)  then instead decided to parade Perderhora on freakshows after forcing him to get a badge and sign a contract (of which some have raised saying it’s not legal.)  
    * During one of those transports passing close to Deltacross, some of the pussy power faction members pounced on it, and freed all the freak show members. During it, Perderhora escaped, and to this day has never been seen again.  
* **Stats**  
  * **Book ? (Arc 2 inset)**  
    * **Age**: 70 (against 1039 A.G)  
    * **Height**: 140cm  
    * **Weight**: 35kg  
* **Soul Energy Capabilities**

  * **Additional Skills**

# **Anpu Sundeath Pharaohs**

These two want to become a single entity so badly they are always on nari gels to look perfectly alike. They even developed a synchronicity interface through eyesight that allows them to predict what each other is thinking nearly instinctively. That is unless a monkey wrench is thrown in their act, like Neferteri showing up or you asking a question that scratches the individualism laying dormant underneath it all. Will they become the next leaders of Sundeath? Eventually, yes, but Gamal does not bulge from the role until they get their act together. However, the Pharaohs guild has no other twin girls for marriage, plus ignoring the rumors that these two brothers only love themselves is hard to do when you see them riding a single Egua together, often galloping.

* **Likes/Dislikes**

  * Hates anything that gets in the way.  
  * If Neferteri was twins, she would have likely married them instead.  
    * Even though Neferteri has not, they both still have feelings for her.  
* **Isekai History (Prior to Story)**  
  * Born as twin and grew very close to his brother. From early childhood, they both were treated like some sort of deity, so they developed a profound narcissism of them being better than anybody else, and the only other person that was as good as the twin brother.  
  * Eventually the narcissistic personality developed into sexual desires as well, which helped the synchronicity of the brothers at the expense of leaving the Sundeath leadership in an impasse which lasted to this day, where one of them will be the new Pharaoh, but they refuse to do so, as they both need to sit equally on the throne. That issue plus the lack of girls in the family that can fulfill their desire also doesn’t help matters.
